### [67] [Geodesics and Thermodynamics of a Schwarzschild Black Hole with Hernquist Dark Matter](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.24046)
*A. R. P. Moreira,A. Bouzenada,F. M. Belchior,F. C. E. Lima*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究了嵌入Hernquist暗物质晕中的Schwarzschild黑洞的物理与几何性质，分析了暗物质对光子轨道、热力学性质及标量扰动的影响，发现暗物质显著改变了黑洞的标准真空解特性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究暗物质晕（特别是Hernquist分布）如何影响黑洞的基本物理性质，包括光传播、热力学行为和场扰动，以理解暗物质与黑洞共存系统的非平凡物理效应。

Method: 将Hernquist暗物质质量分布引入Schwarzschild度规构建修正黑洞度规；求解类光测地线以分析光子轨迹变形；推导质量、视界条件、霍金温度、熵、吉布斯自由能和热容等热力学量；研究标量场在该背景下的微扰演化。

Result: 暗物质晕导致光子路径偏折、热力学结构（如温度、熵、稳定性）发生明显改变，并对标量扰动频谱产生非平庸修正；所有结果均偏离纯Schwarzschild真空解。

Conclusion: Hernquist暗物质晕对黑洞的光学、热力学和动力学性质具有实质性影响，表明在考虑真实天体环境时，必须纳入暗物质效应以获得更准确的黑洞物理描述。

Abstract: In this work, we investigate the physical and geometrical properties of a Schwarzschild black hole (BH) immersed in a Hernquist dark matter halo. To accomplish our purpose, one builds the BH metric by incorporating the Hernquist dark matter profile into the Schwarzschild geometry. In addition, we verify the null geodesic solutions and the Halo effect on photon dynamics. Within this framework, one examines the corresponding light trajectories to determine the deformation of photon paths generated by the dark matter distribution. Furthermore, the thermodynamic properties of the system are studied by deriving expressions for the black hole mass, the horizon condition, the Hawking temperature, the entropy, the Gibbs free energy, and the heat capacity. Our results show that the dark matter halo modifies the thermal structure and stability conditions of the black hole configuration. Finally, we investigate the scalar perturbations to examine the influence of the Hernquist halo on the dynamical propagation of scalar fields in the BH background. In this framework, the results obtained demonstrate that the dark matter parameters yield nontrivial corrections to the optical, thermodynamic, and perturbative properties of the Schwarzschild black hole, producing deviations from the standard vacuum solution.

### [68] [Hawking atmosphere of anti-de Sitter black holes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.24091)
*A. F. Cardona,C. Molina*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究了反德西特（AdS）黑洞霍金大气的半经典演化，结合Parikh-Wilczek隧穿方法与Vaidya-AdS几何下的能量动量张量计算，揭示了小质量AdS黑洞蒸发过程中显著偏离黑体辐射的行为及其热力学与几何耦合机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解渐近AdS时空下黑洞蒸发动力学中几何、量子场与热力学的相互作用，特别是霍金大气的非平衡演化行为。

Method: 采用Parikh-Wilczek隧穿方法建模霍金辐射并计入黑洞质量回响效应；同时在Vaidya-AdS动态几何中计算量子场的重正化能量-动量张量。

Result: 发现小AdS黑洞的时间依赖光度显著偏离理想黑体行为——其光度不随温度升高而增大，源于蒸发过程中强烈的质量变化；两种方法相互印证了熵变、几何演化与辐射谱之间的深层联系。

Conclusion: 霍金大气的演化由黑洞几何动力学、量子隧穿概率及热力学熵变共同决定；在AdS背景下，小黑洞蒸发呈现强非黑体特征，凸显回响效应与边界条件的关键作用。

Abstract: This work investigates the semiclassical evolution of the Hawking atmosphere surrounding evaporating, spherically symmetric anti-de Sitter (adS) black holes. We model the evaporation process within a dynamical framework, treating the emission of Hawking radiation as a quantum tunneling process through the black-hole horizon. Using the Parikh-Wilczek tunneling method, we incorporate backreaction effects, with the emission probability being linked to the resulting change in the Bekenstein-Hawking entropy of the black hole. This probability is then used to compute the time-dependent luminosity of the system, revealing significant deviations from ideal blackbody behavior, particularly for small adS black holes. For these objects, the luminosity does not increase with temperature due to strong mass variations during evaporation. To complement this microscopic approach, we compute the renormalized energy-momentum tensor for a quantum field propagating in the Vaidya-adS geometry modelling the evaporation process. Together, these approaches clarify the interplay between geometry, quantum fields, and thermodynamics in shaping the Hawking atmosphere and the evaporation dynamics of black holes in asymptotically adS spacetimes.

### [69] [Red/Blue shifts of photons in a Hayward black hole immersed in perfect fluid dark matter](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.24102)
*L. Marlene. López,L. A. López*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究了在完美流体暗物质（PFDM）环绕的Hayward正则黑洞周围作稳定圆轨道运动的粒子所发射光子的红移/蓝移特性，并分析了黑洞阴影，探讨其作为PFDM观测特征的潜力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索完美流体暗物质（PFDM）对Hayward正则黑洞周围强引力场中光子频率偏移和黑洞阴影的影响，以寻找PFDM的可观测引力效应。

Method: 理论建模与解析计算：构建含PFDM的Hayward黑洞度规，分析其视界结构、光子球半径、ISCO半径；计算沿稳定圆轨道运动粒子所发射光子的红移/蓝移；推导并分析黑洞阴影半径，并与银河系中心超大质量黑洞Sgr A*的观测约束进行比较。

Result: PFDM参数改变黑洞几何结构：正PFDM参数减小阴影半径，负参数导致更大偏离Schwarzschild情形；红移在纯Hayward情况下最小，随PFDM参数增大而增大，蓝移则相反；频率偏移与阴影特征可作为PFDM存在的潜在观测信号。

Conclusion: 光子红/蓝移及黑洞阴影是探测PFDM在强引力场中效应的有效探针，为未来高精度黑洞观测（如EHT后续计划）提供了理论依据和判据。

Abstract: We investigate the red/blue shifts of photons emitted by particles moving along stable circular orbits around a Hayward regular black hole immersed in perfect fluid dark matter (PFDM). The PFDM contribution modifies the horizon structure and shifts the characteristic radii associated with circular motion, including the photon sphere and the ISCO radius. We show that the redshift reaches its minimum in the pure Hayward case and increases for nonzero values of the PFDM parameter, whereas the blueshift exhibits the opposite behavior. We also analyze the black hole shadow and compare the results with the observational constraints from Sgr A*. Positive values of the PFDM parameter reduce the shadow radius, while negative values produce larger deviations from the Schwarzschild case. These results suggest that frequency shifts and black hole shadows may provide observational signatures of PFDM effects in strong gravitational fields.

### [70] [Probing the limits of the semiclassical Einstein equation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.24103)
*Gustavo Schranck Habermann,Daniel A. Turolla Vanzella*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文提出一种新方法来探测半经典引力近似（即半经典爱因斯坦方程）的适用边界，通过利用引力的非线性特性，在一个可控且解析可解的弱引力混合态模型中，揭示其可导致强引力行为；并借助分支简并可观测量对比量子引力与半经典引力的预测，从而界定后者的有效性范围。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 半经典爱因斯坦方程虽被广泛用于描述量子物质对时空的反作用，但其隐含‘量子涨落小’的假设与应力-能量张量期望值涨落发散的事实存在根本张力，亟需厘清其适用边界。

Method: 构造一个受控、解析可解的弱引力量子态的非相干混合体系，利用引力的固有非线性，诱导系统进入强引力区域；引入分支简并可观测量作为探针，实现量子引力与半经典引力预测的直接比较。

Result: 成功构建出一个理论模型，其中弱引力量子态的统计混合能触发强引力效应，表明半经典近似在此类情形下失效；分支简并可观测量可定量揭示两类理论预测的偏差。

Conclusion: 半经典引力并非普适近似，其有效性高度依赖于量子态的相干结构与引力非线性耦合方式；本文提出的探测框架为实验或数值检验其边界提供了新思路。

Abstract: In the context of semiclassical gravity, the semiclassical Einstein equation is often invoked when backreaction of quantum matter/fields on the spacetime is at stake. It is expected to hold when quantum fluctuations are small. Yet, it is routinely used to justify the central role of the expectation value of the stress-energy tensor of quantum fields, whose fluctuations formally diverge. Here we propose a new way to probe the limits of this approximation by exploiting peculiar nonlinearities of gravity. As a proof of principle, we construct a controlled, analytically tractable setting where the incoherent mixture of weak-gravity states drives the system into a strong-gravity regime. By selecting a branch-degenerate observable, one can compare predictions of quantum and semiclassical gravity, potentially delimiting the validity of the latter.

</details>


### [71] [Towards a causal effective thermodynamics of scalar-tensor gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.24133)
*Narayan Banerjee,Andrea Giusti,Valerio Faraoni,Luca Gallerani,Alain Maltais-Gosselin*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文将标量-张量引力的有效流体与Eckart不可逆热力学的热类比扩展到因果Israel-Stewart模型，通过将热流密度提升为类时矢量，实现了有效温度和有效热导率的首次一致解耦，并保持广义相对论作为平衡态的物理解释。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 扩展热类比至更普适、因果的热力学框架（Israel-Stewart模型），以克服Eckart理论的非因果性缺陷，并实现引力热力学变量的物理分离。

Method: 采用最小假设——将热流密度推广为类时矢量，在Israel-Stewart框架下构建标量-张量引力的有效流体热力学模型，推导可解析的本构方程。

Result: 获得了解析可处理的本构关系，首次一致地解耦了标量-张量引力中的有效温度𝒯和有效热导率𝒦；证明了在𝒦𝒯→0极限下，广义相对论自然恢复为平衡态。

Conclusion: 该因果热力学形式为标量-张量引力提供了更自洽的非平衡热力学描述，并成功应用于宇宙学，增强了引力热力学的理论基础与适用性。

Abstract: The thermal analogy between the effective fluid of scalar-tensor gravity and Eckart's irreversible thermodynamics is extended to the causal Israel-Stewart model, adopting the minimal ansatz of promoting the heat flux density to a timelike vector. This choice yields analytically manageable constitutive equations, allowing for the first consistent decoupling of the effective temperature $\mathcal{T}$ and the effective thermal conductivity $\mathcal{K}$ of scalar-tensor gravity. Crucially, this new framework preserves the interpretation of general relativity as the equilibrium state approached via a dynamical relaxation process in the vanishing-$\mathcal {KT}$ limit. This new causal formalism is applied to cosmology.

### [72] [Inferring Neutron-Star Properties from Post-merger Gravitational-wave Spectra with Neural Networks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.24145)
*Dimitrios Pesios,Nikolaos Stergioulas*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种利用人工神经网络从双中子星并合后的引力波频谱反推中子星物理性质（如质量、潮汐形变率、质量-半径关系斜率）的方法，并在无噪声数值相对论数据上验证了其优于线性模型的性能与物理一致性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解决从双中子星并合后引力波频谱中直接反推中子星物性（如质量、潮汐形变、质量-半径关系）这一非线性逆问题，为未来第三代引力波探测器提供可行的参数提取工具。

Method: 使用无噪声的数值相对论后并合频谱数据，训练三种人工神经网络回归模型（单任务集成、多任务、专家混合）及两种多元线性回归基线；采用两阶段训练策略（残差加权）、结合Dropout、高斯噪声注入和早停等正则化手段构建逆向代理模型。

Result: 神经网络显著优于线性基线；单任务网络集成效果最佳；多任务模型在预测dR/dM上精度相当；专家混合模型揭示了不同频段对参数推断的重要性；最优模型能复现已知经验关系（如主频与潮汐形变关系）并恢复状态方程依赖的趋势。

Conclusion: 神经网络代理模型是未来从真实后并合引力波信号中提取中子星物性的有前途方法，尽管当前结果基于理想无噪声数据。

Abstract: We present a proof-of-concept study of the inverse problem of inferring neutron-star properties directly from the post-merger gravitational-wave spectrum of equal-mass binary neutron-star mergers. Using noise-free spectra from numerical-relativity catalogs, we train and compare three artificial-neural-network regression models and two multivariate linear-regression baselines to predict the stellar mass, $M$, the quadrupolar tidal deformability, $κ_2^τ$, and the slope of the mass--radius relation, $dR/dM$. Since the inverse mapping is nonlinear and cannot be obtained by analytically inverting the direct neural-network model, we construct inverse surrogates and train the networks with a two-stage procedure in which residuals from an initial pass define sample weights for a second pass, together with regularization via dropout, Gaussian-noise injection, and early stopping. We find that neural networks consistently outperform linear baselines, showing that nonlinear surrogates capture the inverse relation between post-merger spectra and source properties more effectively than algebraic inversion. The best performance is achieved by an ensemble of single-task networks, while a multi-task model gives comparable accuracy for predicting the mass--radius slope, and a mixture-of-experts architecture provides insight into spectral-region importance. We further show that the best model reproduces empirical relations between the dominant post-merger frequency and tidal deformability, and recovers equation-of-state-dependent mass--tidal-deformability trends, indicating physical consistency beyond pointwise accuracy. Although restricted to idealized noise-free spectra, the results show that neural-network surrogates provide a promising route for extracting neutron-star information from post-merger signals with future third-generation detectors.

</details>


### [73] [Stress-Energy Tensor for Modified General Relativity with Quantum-Deformed Metric in Riemann Spacetime](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.24282)

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 调和量子力学（QM）与广义相对论（GR），解决二者在基本尺度（如普朗克尺度）上的不兼容问题，特别是引入最小长度不确定性以反映量子引力效应。

Method: 基于广义不确定性原理构建非对易海森堡代数；通过几何量子化构造Finsler流形上带额外曲率的量子形变度规；在Riemann流形上建立无挠量子形变度规，包含最小长度离散化项及切向余矢量二阶导数；修正物质拉格朗日量中的应力-能量张量与电流密度。

Result: 导出了量子诱导的、协变导数为零的修正应力-能量张量；表明经典与量子物质间存在能量动量交换，非引力能量动量不再严格守恒；在最小长度或切向余矢量导数消失时可退化至经典爱因斯坦张量。

Conclusion: 所提出的量子诱导应力-能量张量兼具经典与量子适用性，为统一QM与GR提供了自洽的场源表述框架。

Abstract: The generalized noncommutative Heisenberg algebra, which is based on the generalized uncertainty principle, imposes a minimal length uncertainty on quantum mechanics (QM), on one hand. On the other hand, the quantum-induced spacetime which is based on quantum-deformed metric through geometric quantization is proposed as additional curvatures on the relativistic tangent bundle on Finsler manifold. An additional term that incorporates minimal length discretization along with second-order derivatives of tangent covectors, thereby suggesting an approach to reconcile the principles of QM with General Relativity (GR), is utilized for the construction of a torsion-free quantum-deformed metric on Riemann manifold. Consequently, it is proposed that quantum-induced revisions to the symmetric stress-energy tensor, source of spacetime curvature, along with the current density related to the gauge transformations of gravity, ought to be taken into account in the matter Lagrangian with electromagnetic and scalar components. Vanishing covariant derivative of the quantum-induced stress-energy tensor suggests that the corresponding continuity equation implies that the gravitational fields do work on the classical and quantum matter and vice versa and the non-gravitational energy and momentum are no longer entirely conserved. For vanishing tangent covector derivatives and/or minimal length uncertainty, the classical formulations of the Einstein stress-energy tensor are retained and accordingly that of GR and QM. We conclude that the proposed quantum-induced formulation of the stress-energy tensor is fundamentally suitable for both classical and quantum-induced field equations.

Conclusion: 全斯托克斯分析是SGWB研究的必要扩展，不仅避免强度模型偏差，还能解锁引力波偏振信息这一新探针，对区分不同宇宙学或天体物理起源（如一阶相变、宇宙弦、CBC foreground等）具有关键意义。

Abstract: Gravitational waves admit a Stokes decomposition into intensity ($I$), circular polarization ($V$), and linear polarization ($Q$, $U$), analogous to Cosmic Microwave Background (CMB) polarimetry. Applied to LVK O3 data, we constrain the polarized angular spectra $C^{VV}_\ell$, $C^{EE}_\ell$, $C^{BB}_\ell$ and $|C^{IV}_\ell|$. We show that an intensity-only model is biased when polarized sky components are present, since the detector-network Fisher inner product does not generally make the Stokes responses orthogonal. For transient CBC foregrounds, polarized shot noise is not parametrically suppressed relative to ordinary CBC intensity shot noise. ### [77] [Shaping black hole resonances I. Black hole ringdown as a spectral filtering process](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.24704)
*Alejandro Svyatkovskyy Kholyavka,Jose Antonio León Vega,Samuel Gómez Gómez,Xisco Jiménez Forteza,Sayak Datta*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文揭示了黑洞环down过程中准正规模（QNM）激发的普适谱规则：各模式的激发强度由扰动在该模式特征频率处的傅里叶分量决定；黑洞起着共振谱滤波器作用；作者构造可控局域扰动并开发新拟合工具QNMToolkit验证该机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 准正规模激发的物理机制尚不明确，以往多依赖个案分析，缺乏统一、定量的理论描述。

Method: 基于激发系数的因子分解性质推导谱规则；构造具有可调谱宽和载频的局域扰动；解析推导激发振幅等于初始数据空间傅里叶变换在k∼ω_n处的加权值；结合数值模拟与新开发的QNMToolkit拟合算法，在滑动时窗上进行大量环down拟合并量化拟合方差。

Result: 证实黑洞作为共振谱滤波器，QNM激发强度正比于扰动在对应模式频率处的傅里叶含量；激发在扰动主频接近QNM实部时达最大；数值验证精度达百分之一量级。

Conclusion: QNM激发遵循简单而普适的谱匹配规则，为理解黑洞响应、波形建模及引力波数据分析提供了基础性原理与实用工具。

Abstract: The ringdown of a perturbed black hole (BH) can be described as a superposition of quasinormal modes (QNMs), whose frequencies are determined by the spacetime geometry while their amplitudes depend also on the perturbing source. However, the physical mechanism governing mode excitation remains unclear and is typically treated on a case by case basis. In this work, we show that QNM excitation is governed by a simple spectral rule: each mode is excited according to the Fourier content of the perturbation evaluated at its characteristic frequency. This result follows from the factorization of the excitation coefficients and establishes a direct, quantitative connection between the spectral properties of the perturbation and the resulting ringdown amplitudes. To make this mechanism explicit and controllable, we construct localized perturbations with independently tunable spectral bandwidth and carrier frequency. We demonstrate analytically and numerically that BHs act as resonant spectral filters. We show analytically that the excitation amplitude of each mode equals the weighted spatial Fourier transform of the initial data evaluated at wavenumber $k\simω_n$ so that the filter selectively excites modes whose frequencies lie within the spectral support of the perturbation while suppressing others. Consequently, the excitation is maximized when the dominant perturbation frequency lies close to the real part of the QNM frequency, and we validate this at the percent level with fits to time-domain numerical evolutions. To robustly perform these fits, we have developed a new fitting algorithm, $\mathtt{QNMToolkit}$, which performs ringdown fits over large ensembles of sliding time-domain windows and quantifies the resulting fitting variance.

</details>

Abstract: The physical origin of spacetime discreteness remains a central open problem in quantum gravity, with most existing approaches relying on specific microscopic structures or model-dependent assumptions. In this letter, spacetime discreteness can arise instead as a consequence of consistent microscopic measurement. By treating infinitesimal spacetime intervals as scale-dependent measurement outcomes rather than predefined geometric entities, we formulate a Micro-Measurement Principle in which spacetime quantum fluctuations are encoded directly in the scaling structure. An equivalent dual representation of microscopic lengths leads to discrete, equidistant measurement outcomes, with the corresponding scaling-deformed uncertainty relation thereby reducing to the standard Heisenberg form. The microscopic lengths are further governed by a geometric renormalization-group flow admitting finite-length fixed points. This construction preserves Lorentz invariance and general covariance without ad hoc cutoffs or symmetry breaking. Our results show that the classical continuous-spacetime description corresponds to an unstable limiting regime, whereas a finite microscopic length and a discrete spacetime structure arise naturally from the fundamental requirements of micro-measurement consistency.

The formalism is applied to representative halo profiles, including the Einasto, Dehnen, Burkert, and pseudo-isothermal families. For halo distributions with finite central density, the resulting geometries naturally exhibit de Sitter cores and asymptotically Schwarzschild behavior, providing a controlled and physically transparent link between dark matter halo phenomenology and regular black-hole spacetimes. Result: WKB与准正规模方法结果基本一致，低多极矩处存在微小差异；标量场质量增加会抬高并拓宽势垒，抑制固定频率下的透射，并将高效透射移向更高频；耦合参数显著影响灰体因子和黑洞热力学行为。

Conclusion: 广义Proca理论中的矢量毛黑洞展现出丰富的散射与热力学特性，其行为强烈依赖于测试场质量与相互作用耦合，为检验超越GR的矢量引力模型提供了可观测线索。

Abstract: Generalized Proca theory supplements gravity with a massive vector field whose derivative self-interactions can support black holes carrying primary vector hair. In the asymptotically de Sitter branch considered here, the de Sitter scale is effective: it is generated by the vector sector rather than imposed through a bare cosmological-constant term. We compute grey-body factors and effective absorption cross-sections for massive scalar, electromagnetic, and massless Dirac test fields on this background. The transmission curves are obtained from a sixth-order WKB barrier calculation and are compared with the quasinormal-mode reconstruction; the two descriptions mostly agree, with small visible differences at lower mutlipoles. Increasing the scalar mass raises and broadens the scalar barrier, suppresses transmission at fixed frequency, and shifts efficient transmission to higher frequencies. The couplings considerably affect the grey-body factors and black hole thermodynamics.

</details>


### [81] [Chaotic motion of particles around a Schwarzschild black hole in a swirling electromagnetic background](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.25094)

Method: 采用庞加莱截面、最大李雅普诺夫指数、快速李雅普诺夫指示器、重现性分析和分岔图等动力学诊断工具。

Abstract: We investigate the particle motion around a Schwarzschild black hole immersed in a swirling Bertotti-Robinson-Bonnor-Melvin background. This spacetime provides a physically well-motivated framework for studying how the two different electromagnetic components and the swirling deformation affect particle dynamics near compact objects. By employing Poincaré sections, the maximum Lyapunov exponent, the Fast Lyapunov indicator, recurrence analysis and bifurcation diagrams, we show that chaotic motion can already appear in the non-swirling Schwarzschild-Bertotti-Robinson black hole. This indicates that the swirling background is not a necessary condition for chaos in this family of spacetimes, it mainly shifts the parameter region where chaos occurs. We further find that the effects of the two electromagnetic fields are very complicated. In particular, the existence of bound orbits is strongly restricted by the strengths of the two electromagnetic fields and their relative direction. These results provide rich numerical evidence that the chaotic motion of particles is associated with the nonlinear interaction between the accessible phase space, the electromagnetic backreaction and the swirling deformation.

### [82] [Gravitational Wave Propagation in K-essence Cosmology: Theory and Observational Constraints](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.25466)
*Sougata Bhunia,Eduardo Guendelman,Debashis Gangopadhyay,Ramón Herrera,Abhijit Bhattacharyya,Goutam Manna*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 在FLRW背景下采用高频近似，聚焦横迹自由张量扰动，推导k-essence中引力波的修正演化方程；构建红移依赖的有效质量m_eff(z)；通过贝叶斯联合分析CC、BAO、Pantheon+SH0ES及GWTC-2.1/3/4标准汽笛数据进行检验。

Result: 引力波传播速度严格为光速；出现背景诱导的有效质量项m_eff(z)，导致累积相位偏移但不引入新自由度；m_eff(z)由宇宙学参数唯一确定；联合数据分析支持该模型，且其演化趋势有助于缓解H₀张力。

Abstract: Gravitational waves (GWs) provide a powerful, theory-independent probe of the dynamical structure of spacetime and the cosmological background. We study linearized GW propagation in k-essence cosmology, where a non-canonical scalar field describes the dark sector. In the high-frequency (short-wavelength) approximation on a Friedmann--Lemaître--Robertson--Walker (FLRW) background, and restricting to the transverse-traceless tensor sector, we derive a modified evolution equation for tensor perturbations. The GW speed remains strictly luminal, consistent with multimessenger bounds such as GW170817, but the interaction with the background field $\barφ$ induces a time-dependent effective mass-like term $m_{\rm eff}$. This background-induced mass modifies the dispersion relation without introducing additional propagating degrees of freedom, leading to a cumulative, frequency-dependent phase shift in the waveform over cosmological distances. We show that $m_{\rm eff}$ is uniquely determined by background cosmological parameters and can be written as a redshift-dependent function, $m_{\rm eff}(z)$, directly linking GW observables to scalar-field dynamics, while the GW luminosity distance remains identical to its electromagnetic counterpart, preserving standard-siren consistency. We test the scenario through a joint Bayesian analysis that combines cosmic chronometers (CC), BAO, Pantheon+SH0ES, and standard-siren data from GWTC-2.1/3/4. The reconstruction is consistent with current constraints and reproduces the late-time expansion history, while the evolution of $m_{\rm eff}(z)$ offers a new mechanism that may help alleviate the $H_0$ tension.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 场质量增大导致总吸收截面减小；散射谱中干涉峰宽度随场质量增大而变宽（当波速>v_c时）；在低至近极值电荷下，有质量场可使正则与标准黑洞的吸收/散射谱趋于一致。

Abstract: Regular black holes (RBHs) can be seen as possible alternatives to standard black holes (BHs), since these geometries do not have a curvature singularity. As a way of improving our knowledge of such geometries, we can investigate how the astrophysical environment interacts with RBHs and compare the results with those obtained in the framework of standard BHs. In this work, we aim to study the absorption and scattering cross sections of massive scalar waves impinging on Ayón-Beato-García and Bardeen charged RBH geometries, focusing on understanding the role played by the field's mass. Concerning the absorption spectrum, our numerical results show that the total absorption cross section decreases as we increase the field's mass for fixed values of the BH charge. In turn, in the scattering spectrum, an increase in the mass of the field leads to wider interference widths for field velocities larger than a critical value, $v_c$. Moreover, we also compare our numerical results with the classical and semiclassical approximations, showing that they agree very well within the appropriate limits. We also draw comparisons with the results of the Reissner-Nordström metric. In particular, we show that the mass of the field contributes to finding situations in which the absorption and scattering spectra of regular and standard BHs are similar for arbitrary values of the field frequency and scattering angle, considering low- to near-extreme BH charges.

The spacetime geometry contains, in addition to the Schwarzschild mass term, a quintessence contribution controlled by the intensity parameter $N$ and the state parameter $ω_q$, an exponential hair correction governed by the coupling $α$ and the primary hair scale $\ell$, and a cosmological constant $Λ$. We first examined the horizon structure and derived the black hole mass from the horizon condition. The Hawking temperature, heat capacity, and Gibbs free energy were then analyzed in order to identify the influence of the hair and surrounding-field parameters on local and global thermodynamic behavior. The results show that the exponential hair mainly affects the small-horizon regime, while the quintessential sector and the cosmological constant produce significant changes in the large-scale behavior of the black hole. In particular, the heat capacity exhibits divergences associated with second-order phase transitions, and the Gibbs free energy reveals the possibility of competing thermodynamic branches. We also analyzed the sparsity of Hawking radiation and showed that the emitted flux is highly intermittent rather than continuous. The sparsity parameter is controlled by the combination of the Hawking temperature, the effective emitting area, and the greybody factors. Finally, we studied massless scalar perturbations in this background by reducing the Klein-Gordon equation to a radial equation with an effective potential.

### [85] [On the boundary cost of source-consistent warp shells](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.25417)
*An T. Le*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究了亚光速、正能量翘曲壳的经典能量条件可接受性，发现能量条件失效局限于平滑源-真空过渡区域而非内部体区；通过引入两种‘源优先’壳模型并应用五准则标准评估八种翘曲驱动构造，均未完全达标；尽管内部能量条件基本满足，但在平滑尾部出现Hawking-Ellis IV型违反；大量参数扫描未找到符合条件的构型，且边界缺陷与过渡几何相关；沿类光射线的零能量线积分始终为正，提示点态违反未必影响平均零能量条件。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 回应Barzegar、Buchert和Vigneron对翘曲驱动模型源一致性问题的批评，建立严格、帧无关的能量条件评估标准，系统检验亚光速正能量翘曲壳是否真正满足物理可接受性要求。

Method: 提出两种‘源优先’翘曲壳试探解（无位移S-shell和由动量约束导出位移的T-shell），基于爱因斯坦约束从预设物质模型反推度规势；构建包含正则性、约束满足性、显式物质模型、帧无关能量条件余量及全局诊断的五准则评估标准；对八类典型翘曲驱动构造进行系统检验，并开展600组壳紧凑度与厚度参数扫描；辅以独立帧无关验证（如Fuchs匀速壳）及类光射线零能量线积分分析。

Result: 所有被检构造均未通过全部五项准则；Fuchs匀速壳内部能量条件高度满足（13个探针中仅0个违反），但平滑尾部存在Hawking-Ellis Type IV型违反；600组参数扫描无一满足全部条件；边界能量条件缺陷在无位移S-shell及其静态极限（v₀=0）下均存在，表明其源于过渡几何而非位移效应；沿代表性离轴类光射线，所有源设定壳的零能量线积分均为正。

Conclusion: 当前主流亚光速正能量翘曲壳模型在严格的源一致性和帧无关能量条件框架下仍不可行；能量条件失效本质定位于源-真空平滑过渡区域，提示需重构该几何界面的物理建模；零能量线积分为正的结果虽不构成ANEC证明，但暗示点态违反可能被平均抵消，为后续研究提供新线索。

Abstract: We study classical energy-condition admissibility for subluminal, positive-energy warp shells. For the constructions examined here, the energy-condition failures are localized at the smooth source--vacuum transition rather than in the bulk interior. We introduce two \emph{source-first} shell ans"atze whose metric potentials are obtained from the Einstein constraints for a prescribed matter model: a shift-free S-shell and a T-shell whose shift is derived from the momentum constraint. We assess them with a five-criterion standard comprising regularity, constraint satisfaction, an explicit matter model, frame-independent energy-condition margins, and global diagnostics; the standard responds to the source-consistency critique of Barzegar, Buchert, and Vigneron. Applied to eight constructions spanning the canonical warp-drive classes, none passes the full standard. An independent frame-independent verification of the Fuchs constant-velocity shell confirms interior energy-condition compliance (0 of 13 interior probes violate) but reveals Hawking--Ellis Type~IV violations in the smoothing tail beyond the nominal shell. A frame-independent scan over shell compactness and thickness (600 configurations) yields no admissible configuration in either source-first class. The same boundary deficit appears in the shift-free S-shell and persists in the static $v_0=0$ limit, which ties it to the transition geometry rather than to the shift. Along a representative off-axis null ray the null-energy line integral is nevertheless positive for every source-prescribed shell; this is an exploratory diagnostic rather than a proof of the averaged null energy condition, but it shows that the pointwise boundary failures need not appear in that integral.

### [86] [A New Self-Dual Gravitational Instanton Solution on a Local Conformal Kählerian Manifold in a Brane World Model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.25532)
*Reinoud Jan Slagter*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文发现了一个在共形稀释子引力中真空Kerr-like翘曲时空上的精确引力瞬子解，该解源于一阶偏微分方程，具有自对偶性；奇点由五次多项式决定，超出Plebanski-Demianski分类（四次）；解对应于一个有效四维自对偶Kähler流形，具循环共形结构；通过5D到膜的Weyl张量投影实现；拓扑为S³×ℝ/ℤ₂，并利用Klein瓶上的对跖边界条件与Hopf纤维化描述霍金辐射，避免信息超距传输；最后指出其内部结构与Janis-Newman-Winicour复坐标模型存在联系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索超越标准黑洞分类（如Plebanski-Demianski）的新引力瞬子解，构建具自对偶性、良好奇点结构及物理合理霍金辐射机制的共形稀释子引力模型。

Conclusion: 该工作拓展了黑洞瞬子的数学分类与几何理解，表明五次奇点多项式是Petrov D型轴对称情形的上限；确立了共形结构、Kähler几何与霍金辐射量子纯性之间的新桥梁；为量子引力中信息守恒问题提供了几何化新视角。

Abstract: An exact gravitational instanton solution on a vacuum Kerr-like warped spacetime in conformal dilaton gravity is found. Remarkably, the metric solution results from a first-order PDE, allowing the connection with self-duality. The singular points are determined by a quintic polynomial. This suggests that this is the highest possible polynomial in describing the singularities of black holes of Petrov type D axially symmetric manifolds and don't fits the Plebanski-Demianski classification of black holes which is determined by a fourth order polynomial. The solution can be described by a locally conformal Kählerian manifold with Euclidean signature and a Kähler potential. This is possible for the effective 4D manifold, despite the fact that a Kähler manifold in 5D cannot be modelled. We are dealing with an effective 4D self-dual Kähler manifold with a recurrent conformal structure. This happened by the projected Weyl tensor of 5D on the brane. The topology of the gravitational instanton would be $S^3\times \mathbb{R}/\mathbb{Z}_2$. The antipodal boundary condition on the hyper-surface of a Klein bottle $\sim \mathbb{C}^1\times\mathbb{C}^1$ is applied to describe the Hawking particles during the evaporation process. We used the Hopf fibration to get $S^2$ as the black hole horizon, where the centrix is not in a torus but in the Klein bottle. The twist fits very well with the antipodal identification of the points on the horizon. No 'cut and past' is necessary, so the Hawing particles remain pure without instantaneous information transport. Finally, we reveal a connection between the description of the interior of our new black hole solution and the similar model proposed by Janis, Newman and Winicour some time ago of the Schwarzschild solution in complex coordinates with a zero rest mass scalar field, which develops an anomalous asymmetry.

### [87] [A pre-merger-informed spectral-level ringdown inference framework for black-hole spectroscopy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.25623)
*Shitong Guo,Yan-Gang Miao*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文提出SPRING框架，旨在将引力波环-down信号的准正规模（QNM）谱推断与理论模型解耦，并利用并合前数据提升振幅估计，从而实现更纯粹的黑洞光谱学分析。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有黑洞光谱学方法常将QNM谱测量与特定理论（如Kerr）参数推断混杂；且传统环-down分析忽略并合前数据中蕴含的QNM激发振幅与相位信息。

Method: 提出SPRING框架，采用无先验理论假设的双分量阻尼正弦波（2DS）模型，在谱层面进行环-down推断，并将并合前信息通过振幅尺度估计传递至环-down分析中。

Result: 在GW250114事件中应用SPRING，相比不使用并合前信息的方法，贝叶斯证据提升Δln B ∼ 5–10；尽管引入额外自由度，所得残余黑洞后验分布仍与IMR估计高度一致。

Conclusion: SPRING成功桥接并合前信息与环-down谱推断，为未来无模型依赖的黑洞光谱学提供了完整、谱级的分析路径。

Abstract: Black-hole spectroscopy aims to infer properties of the remnant spacetime from the quasinormal-mode (QNM) spectrum of the gravitational-wave ringdown signal. In most implementations, however, this inference is performed with waveform models that already incorporate Kerr or other theory-specific QNM spectral relations, thereby entangling spectral measurement with remnant or beyond-Kerr parameter inference. At the same time, conventional ringdown analyses commonly excise the pre-merger data, which in principle contain information about the excitation amplitudes and phases of the QNMs. We introduce \texttt{SPRING} (\textit{Spectral-level Pre-merger-informed RINGdown inference}), a framework designed to separate ringdown spectral inference from theory-side interpretation while propagating pre-merger information through amplitude-scale estimation. As a demonstration, we apply \texttt{SPRING} to GW250114 using an agnostic two-component damped-sinusoid (2DS) model for Kerr remnant inference. \texttt{SPRING} improves the Bayesian support for the agnostic 2DS signal model relative to analyses that do not use pre-merger information, with an increase of \(Δ\ln B\sim 5\)--\(10\). The resulting remnant posterior remains closely consistent with the inspiral-merger-ringdown estimate, despite the extra freedom introduced by the second DS component. This work bridges pre-merger information and ringdown inference, establishing a fully spectral-level route for future black-hole spectroscopy.

</details>


### [88] [Periodic orbits and gravitational waveforms around a Schwarzschild black hole with a cloud of strings embedded in perfect fluid dark matter](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.25625)
*Ziqiang Cai,Zhi Li,Zhenglong Ban,Qi-Qi Liang,Zheng-Wen Long*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究了弦云和完美流体暗物质环境下施瓦西黑洞周围粒子轨道动力学及其引力波特征，发现弦云参数a和暗物质参数α对边际束缚轨道（MBO）和最内稳定圆轨道（ISCO）有相反影响，并揭示a增大导致引力波形显著相位延迟。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索弦云和暗物质共同影响下黑洞周围粒子轨道及引力波特征，以区分不同致密天体环境的观测信号。

Method: 理论建模与数值分析：构建含弦云参数a和暗物质参数α的修正施瓦西度规，系统计算MBO、ISCO的半径、能量和角动量，并模拟不同q值周期轨道产生的引力波形。

Result: 1) MBO和ISCO半径及角动量随a增大而增大、随α增大而减小；能量变化趋势相反；2) 弦云参数a增大导致引力波形明显相位延迟，且振幅特征可区分于纯施瓦西情形。

Conclusion: 弦云和暗物质参数对黑洞周边轨道结构和引力波信号具有可观测的差异化影响，为利用引力波探测致密天体周围介质成分提供理论依据。

Abstract: In this study, we explore the dynamics of particle orbits and their corresponding gravitational wave signatures in the vicinity of a Schwarzschild black hole (BH) surrounded by a cloud of strings and embedded in a perfect fluid dark matter medium. The model is characterized by two parameters: $a$, associated with the string cloud, and $α$, representing the dark matter distribution. We systematically analyze how the marginally bound orbit (MBO) and the innermost stable circular orbit (ISCO) depend on these parameters. Our findings reveal that while both the orbital radius and angular momentum increase with increasing $a$, they decrease as $α$ increases; notably, the energy exhibits the opposite trend, decreasing with $a$ and increasing with $α$. Furthermore, we examine periodic orbits indexed by rational numbers $q$ and the gravitational waveforms they generate. The results demonstrate that an increase in the string cloud parameter $a$ induces a significant phase delay in the waveform. Specifically, waveforms with lower values of $a$ oscillate over shorter time intervals, whereas those with higher values extend to longer time scales. These distinct features, including noticeable differences in amplitude, allow the waveforms to be clearly distinguished from those in a pure Schwarzschild spacetime.

### [89] [Scalarization of dark matter stars](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.25671)
*Junya Tanaka*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索标量-张量理论中暗物质星是否会发生自发标量化，并评估其作为标量场与暗物质耦合探针的潜力。

Method: 在标量-张量理论框架下，分析标量场同时耦合重子物质与自相互作用暗物质的情形，数值求解暗物质星结构方程，扫描耦合参数空间（特别是暗物质耦合参数β_d），判断标量场增长（即标量化）发生的条件。

Result: 发现当暗物质耦合参数β_d为负时，标量化在绝大多数参数区域内发生，且该有效参数范围比传统中子星更宽；所涉暗物质参数与解决星系形成问题的自相互作用暗物质模型一致。

Conclusion: 暗物质星比中子星更易发生标量化，若其真实存在，将成为检验标量场-暗物质耦合机制的独特天体实验室。

Abstract: We investigated scalarization in dark matter stars. In scalar tensor theories, the coupling between matter and a scalar field generates an effective mass, which is known to trigger the growth of the scalar field in stars and black holes (spontaneous scalarization). On the other hand, models in which the scalar field couples not only to baryonic matter but also to dark matter have been discussed in the literature. Moreover, in models with self interacting dark matter, it is known that dark matter can form compact objects. Within the framework of scalar tensor theories, we studied the parameter ranges in which the growth of the scalar field occurs in compact stars formed by self interacting dark matter. As a result, we found that scalarization occurs over most of the parameter region with a negative coupling parameter $β_d$. This parameter range is broader than that for scalarization in conventional neutron stars. Since the dark matter parameters considered correspond to those in which self-interacting dark matter resolves problems in galaxy formation, if dark matter stars actually exist, they could serve as probes for investigating the relationship between the scalar field and dark matter.

### [90] [Cesàro convergence of the high-order WKB method and its applications to black-hole overtones and long-lived modes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.25705)
*Roman A. Konoplya,Jerzy Matyjasek,Alexander Zhidenko*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文开发了一种基于Bender-Wu算法的高阶黑洞WKB方法的全自动Mathematica实现，结合对角Padé逼近和Cesàro均值，提升了对难处理模式（如n>l的前几个泛音和大质量场的长寿命准正规模）的计算效率，并提出Cesàro均值单调性可作为WKB方法收敛性的内部判据。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准低阶WKB方法在处理前几个泛音（n>l）和大质量场的长寿命准正规模时效率低下，需发展高阶、自动、稳定的计算方法。

Method: 基于Bender-Wu算法构建全自动Mathematica高阶WKB程序；采用对角/近对角Padé逼近提升精度；引入Cesàro均值分析收敛行为；检验不同黑洞度规（尤其是非适度类）下的WKB序列表现。

Result: 高阶WKB+Padé在两类难题上显著提升效率；发现WKB序列可能虚假收敛，仅数值稳定不足以为正确性判据；Cesàro均值在足够高阶后呈现单调收敛，可作内部收敛判据。

Conclusion: 高阶WKB结合Padé与Cesàro均值是一种有力工具，但其适用性受限于黑洞度规性质；Cesàro单调性是更可靠的内部收敛指标，优于单纯依赖数值稳定。

Abstract: We develop a fully automatic Mathematica implementation of the black-hole WKB method at very high orders based on the Bender-Wu algorithm, which in principle is limited only by memory and computational time, and show that when pushed to sufficiently high order and improved by diagonal Padé approximants the method becomes efficient for two regimes which are usually regarded as difficult for the standard low-order WKB treatment: the first several overtones with n>l and the very long-lived quasinormal modes of massive fields. At the same time, we show that this efficiency has a nontrivial limitation: for black-hole metrics belonging to the non-moderate class, especially when higher coefficients of the near-horizon parametrization become large, the WKB sequence may exhibit an apparent convergence to values which are nevertheless far from the accurate quasinormal frequencies. Thus, numerical stabilization of the WKB output alone is not always a sufficient criterion of correctness. However, we observe that although the WKB method with diagonal or near-diagonal Padé approximants does not exhibit monotonic convergence order by order, the corresponding Cesàro means become monotonically convergent once a sufficiently high WKB order is reached. This behavior may serve as an internal WKB criterion for the convergence of the method.

Abstract: We investigate static, spherically symmetric (SS) spacetimes in covariant teleparallel \(F(T)\) gravity in the presence of electromagnetic sources. A general reconstruction procedure is established, allowing the systematic construction of nonlinear teleparallel \(F(T)\) models for arbitrary coframe ansätze. ### [93] [Generalising gravitationally induced decoherence beyond linear environmental interactions in a microscopic quantum mechanical toy model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.25936)
*Max Joseph Fahn,Renata Ferrero,Kristina Giesel,Roman Kemper*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文推广了Xu和Blencowe（2022）及Domi等（2024）提出的引力诱导退相干量子玩具模型，将环境与系统间相互作用由位置算符的线性耦合推广为基于Weyl元素的耦合，动机源于聚合物量子力学及非线性相互作用构造；通过两种互补解析方法计算环境关联函数，验证了马尔可夫近似有效性，并在Weyl参数小展开下恢复原有线性模型，最终求解了重整化主方程。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 受聚合物量子力学中Weyl元素作为基本算符的启发，以及通过截断指数型Weyl元构造非线性相互作用的可能性，作者将原有线性位置耦合推广为Weyl元素形式的耦合。

Method: 提出基于Weyl元素（特别是正弦型）的系统-环境相互作用模型；发展两种解析计算环境关联函数的方法：一是结合热态Wick定理与升降算符，二是基于短时傅里叶变换、避免使用升降算符以利于推广至聚合物量子化；推广谱密度形式，并利用Weyl参数的小量展开进行分析。

Result: 两种方法得出完全一致的环境关联函数；数值显示其随时间快速衰减，支持马尔可夫近似；一阶Weyl参数展开精确复现Xu-Blencowe与Domi等的原有退相干模型；成功导出并求解了重整化主方程。

Conclusion: Weyl元素耦合是线性耦合的合理推广，兼具理论基础（聚合物量子力学）与物理可实现性（非线性截断），所建立的框架更普适，且在适当极限下能还原已有结果，为主方程建模和退相干机制研究提供了新路径。

Abstract: We generalise the quantum mechanical toy model for gravitationally induced decoherence presented in Xu, Blencowe (2022) and Domi et al. (2024). In contrast to earlier formulations, in which the Hamiltonian of the system of interest is linearly coupled to the position operators of the oscillators in the environment, we consider an interaction formulated in terms of Weyl elements of the environment's position operators. This extension is motivated by polymer quantum mechanics, in which Weyl elements are fundamental operators, as well as by the possibility of generating non-linear interactions through suitable truncations of the exponential Weyl elements. Here we focus on a sinus-like coupling that is still quantised using the Schrödinger representation and, in the limit of a small Weyl parameter, reproduces the conventional linear interaction. To derive the corresponding master equation, we developed two complementary methods for the analytical calculation of the environmental correlation functions. The first utilises Wick's theorem for thermal expectation values in conjunction with annihilation and creation operators, while the second is based on the short-time Fourier transform and completely avoids the use of annihilation and creation operators, making it more readily transferable and generalisable to a polymer quantisation. Both approaches yield identical results. We further generalise the spectral density required for the exponential coupling structure. A numerical analysis shows that the environmental correlation functions decay rapidly with time, which supports the validity of the Markov approximation. Using a Taylor expansion in the Weyl parameter, we show that the first-order term reproduces the decoherence model of Xu, Blencowe (2022) and Domi et al. (2024). Finally, we derive the solution to the renormalised master equation.

### [95] [Hyperboloidal evolution for scalar scattering in Minkowski space](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26028)
*Ekrem S Demirboğa,Anıl Zenginoğlu*

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种在闵可夫斯基时空中的标量波全局散射的时域数值框架，通过精确共形匹配三个紧化区域（过去、空间无穷邻域、未来双曲面域），实现从I⁻到I⁺的无边界全局演化，并在球对称标量波模型中验证了其稳定性与收敛性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 构建基于共形紧化的三区域（过去超曲面域、Penrose域覆盖i⁰、未来超曲面域）精确匹配框架，匹配面为相邻坐标系中相同的共形超曲面；在球对称情形下实现自由传播、线性散射势（如Pöschl–Teller势）及多种非线性（三次、五次、七次）标量波方程的数值求解。

Result: 数值实验表明：跨匹配界面传播稳定；可直接在I⁺提取辐射；自由与线性势情形达四阶收敛；五次与七次非线性情形近似四阶收敛并复现预期晚期尾项；三次非线性仅呈一阶收敛，暴露紧化边界处非零共形源导致的正则性问题。

Abstract: We develop a time-domain numerical framework for global scalar wave scattering in Minkowski spacetime. The main contribution is an exact conformal matching of three compactified regions: a past hyperboloidal domain attached to $\mathscr I^-$, a Penrose domain covering a neighborhood of spatial infinity $i^0$, and a future hyperboloidal domain attached to $\mathscr I^+$. The matching surfaces are identical conformal hypersurfaces in the adjacent charts. This yields a global evolution scheme connecting $\mathscr I^-$, the neighborhood of $i^0$, and $\mathscr I^+$ without artificial timelike outer boundaries and without interpolation between scri-fixing gauges.
  We implement the construction for spherically symmetric scalar waves, including free propagation, localized linear scattering potentials such as the Pöschl--Teller potential, and semilinear wave equations with cubic, quintic, and septic nonlinearities. The numerical experiments demonstrate stable propagation across the matching interfaces, direct extraction of radiation at $\mathscr I^+$, and fourth-order convergence for the free and linear-potential tests. The quintic and septic nonlinear tests exhibit approximately fourth-order convergence and recover the expected late-time tail rates. The cubic case, by contrast, shows only first-order convergence, revealing a limitation of our treatment near compactified boundaries when the conformally rescaled nonlinear source remains non-vanishing. These results validate the conformal matching strategy for long-time simulations, while identifying the boundary regularity issues that must be addressed using a more robust treatment of spatial infinity.

### [96] [Ringdown and echoes from compact objects: Debye series and Debye quasinormal modes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15429)

Method: 构建类Debye展开的波形级数分解，将时空中的标量场响应按几何光学路径（外部传播、表面反射、内部多次透射）分离；结合各Debye项的QNM谱分析，建立Debye-QNM描述；在两类Schwarzschild星模型（R>3M中子星类与R<3M超致密星）上数值验证。

Result: Debye重建高度吻合精确波形，且在早期即收敛；中子星模型中低阶Debye项主导环降与亚阈值支割贡献；超致密模型中Debye级数清晰分离出提示响应、环降及一系列分立的回声波包；Debye-QNM与标准QNM具有互补谱解释：前者对应单通道模式，后者为前者的重求和集体共振。

Conclusion: Debye-QNM框架不仅弥补了标准QNM在早期时间失效的缺陷，还从传播路径角度阐明了回声结构的产生机制以及极点与支割在时域信号中的作用，为致密天体引力波建模与观测解释提供了新范式。

Abstract: We introduce a new series decomposition of the waveform constructed in the spirit of Debye expansions in scattering theory, and we use this to analyse the time-domain response of compact, horizonless bodies to scalar-field perturbations on curved spacetimes. The Debye decomposition separates out direct exterior propagation, surface reflection, and successive transmissions through the interior of a compact body, and it provides an intuitive interpretation of the waveform in terms of geodesic trajectories. By analysing the quasinormal-mode (QNM) content of individual Debye terms, we set out a Debye-QNM description that is complementary to the standard QNM description. With this framework, we examine a scalar field propagating on two illustrative `Schwarzschild star' compact-body spacetimes: a neutron-star-like model \(R>3M\) and an ultracompact object \(R<3M\). We show that the Debye reconstruction matches well with the exact waveform, and that (unlike the standard QNM reconstruction) it converges even at early times, giving an accurate description of all waveform features including the prompt response. In the neutron-star case, the low-order Debye terms mainly describe the ringdown and a non-modal component associated with the sub-threshold branch cut. In the ultracompact case, the Debye series organizes the waveform into a prompt/ringdown contribution followed by a succession of individually resolved echo-like wavepackets. The new Debye-QNM expansion and the standard QNM expansion have complementary spectral interpretations: the former identifies modes in individual propagation channels, whereas the latter describes collective resonances that are resummations of the former. This distinction clarifies how echo-like structures emerge from repeated interior propagation, and how pole and branch-cut contributions enter the time-domain signal.

</details>

### [97] [FASTAR -- I. Continuous and differentiable evolutionary stellar population models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.24093)
*Ignacio Martín-Navarro,Alexandre Vazdekis,Luis Peralta de Arriba,Isaac Alonso Asensio,Eirini Angeloudi,Patricia Iglesias Navarro,Francesco La Barbera,Katja Fahrion,Tereza Jerabkova,Michael A. Beasley,Jesús Falcón-Barroso,Marc Huertas-Company,Sebastián F. Sánchez,Prashin Jethwa*

Main category: astro-ph.GA

TL;DR: FASTAR是一个完全可微分的恒星种群合成代码，能够连续评估任意年龄、金属丰度和初始质量函数（IMF）下的单恒星种群模型，具有高精度、高灵活性和高效性，并支持梯度下降推断算法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统基于网格的恒星种群模型在连续参数空间建模和与反演算法兼容性方面存在局限，限制了从观测数据中提取精确物理信息的能力。

Method: 开发了FASTAR——一个完全可微分的恒星种群合成代码，支持在年龄（20 Myr–14 Gyr）、金属丰度（[M/H] = −2.5 到 +0.3）和IMF参数空间内连续插值与评估；提供MILES波段高分辨率光谱预测及宽波段（2000–12000 Å）粗粒度SED，并支持任意测光滤光片卷积。

Result: FASTAR在拟合球状星团和早型星系高信噪比光谱方面达到当前最先进模型水平，同时更快速、轻量、灵活；其可微性支持不确定性量化和基于梯度下降的参数推断。

Conclusion: FASTAR为恒星种群建模提供了兼具精度、效率与可微性的新范式，显著提升了星系观测数据的物理反演能力。

Abstract: The development of evolutionary stellar population models is central to interpreting observations of galaxies in terms of astrophysical quantities. Stellar population models must therefore be both accurate and compatible with inversion algorithms in order to extract meaningful information from the observed data. Here we present FASTAR, a fully differentiable stellar population synthesis code. Contrary to traditional, grid-based single stellar population models, FASTAR can be continuously evaluated at any age (between 20 Myr and 14 Gyr), metallicity (-2.5 < [M/H] < +0.3), and initial mass function (IMF). Changes in the IMF parameterization are straightforward, allowing for consistent conversions of colors, magnitudes, and mass-to-light ratios, as well as the synthesis of models under the assumption of arbitrary IMF functional forms. FASTAR provides detailed spectroscopic predictions over the MILES wavelength range (3,540-7,400 A) as well as more coarsely sampled spectral energy distributions across a wider 2,000-to-12,000 A, which can be directly convolved with any arbitrary set of photometric filters. FASTAR performs at the same level of state-of-the-art simple stellar population models benchmarked against observations of globular clusters and high signal-to-noise spectra of early-type galaxies, but it is faster, lighter, and more flexible. Moreover, its differentiable nature allows for a quantitative understanding of model behavior and uncertainties, as well as a natural framework for gradient descent inference algorithms.

</details>


### [98] [The AGORA High-resolution Galaxy Simulations Comparison Project. XI: Solving the Non-Spherical Morphology and Evolution of Dark Matter Halos with Haskap Pie](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.24097)
*Kirk S. S. Barrow,Thinh Huu Nguyen,Santi Roca-Fàbrega,Ji-hoon Kim,Varun Satish,Kentaro Nagamine,Saulius Matusaitis,Eduárd Illes,Ramón Rodríguez-Cardoso,Minyong Jung,Hyeonyong Kim,Anna Genina,Pablo Granizo,Alessandro Lupi,Johnny W. Powell,Héctor Velázquez,Tom Abel,Oscar Agertz,Renyue Cen,Daniel Ceverino,Boon Kiat Oh,Yuri Oku,Joel R. Primack,Thomas R. Quinn,Yves Revaz,Alvaro Segovia-Otero,Ikkoh Shimizu,Edward Skrabacz,Romain Teyssier*

Main category: astro-ph.GA

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于非球形假设的暗物质晕求解与追踪新方法，并在CosmoRun模拟中验证了其对形态学特征（如自转、轴比、过密等）的敏感性，揭示了不同数值代码间因并合时机和动力学状态差异导致的形态学差异。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统暗物质晕分析常假设球对称，但实际晕是非球形的；需发展能反映真实形态的分析方法，并在多代码对比框架（AGORA/CosmoRun）中检验形态学趋势的一致性与差异性。

Method: 引入基于Haskap Pie中束缚粒子搜索技术的非球形晕识别与追踪流程，计算多种形态与动力学量（如自转、轴比、过密度），并在CosmoRun多代码水动力学模拟中进行系统比较。

Result: 发现高质比并合显著影响形态指标；代码间最大差异源于并合时间与并合前晕的动力学状态；自转与轴比在4>z>2达峰后下降；过密度兼具质量与红移依赖性，低质量晕在低红移时显著偏离；多数趋势跨代码一致，且偏离位力定理。

Conclusion: 所提非球形方法为暗物质晕形态演化提供了新视角，揭示了以往球对称假设下被掩盖的重要物理趋势，强调了形态学分析中放弃球对称假设的必要性。

Abstract: We introduce a halo solving and tracking procedure that intrinsically treats dark matter halos as non-spherical objects by leveraging the bound particle searching techniques used in Haskap Pie. The AGORA Collaboration's hydrodynamic simulation CosmoRun}project provides a useful laboratory to explore trends in dark matter halo morphology that are revealed by our new procedure in the context of any dispersions or similarities between the codes. We find that several morphological and shape measures were very responsive to high mass ratio mergers. The greatest difference in these measures between the simulation codes were related to timing discrepancies and the dynamical state of the halos prior to the mergers. Most other quantities were similar across codes, including several secular and redshift-dependent trends in various dynamical quantities that showed a departure from Virial Theorem (e.g., overdensity and halo mass). We find that halo spin and the ratio between the semi-major and the semi-minor axis peaked at 4>z>2 before declining at low redshift. Also, halo overdensity is both mass-dependent and redshift-dependent, diverging for low mass halos at low redshift. Our method contributes a new perspective on these trends that have not been fully replicated in other works due to our emphasis on fundamentally non-spherical halos and measures of morphology that correspondingly do not assume spherical symmetry.

</details>


### [99] [Dark matter-deficient twins: FCC 224 and FCC 240 as possible analogues of NGC 1052-DF2 and DF4](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.24099)
*Maria Luisa Buzzo,Pieter van Dokkum,Michael Hilker,Duncan A. Forbes,Aaron J. Romanowsky,Yimeng Tang*

Main category: astro-ph.GA

TL;DR: 本文通过VLT/MUSE光谱观测分析Fornax星系团外围的超弥散星系FCC 224与FCC 240，发现其动力学特征（低速度弥散、暗物质缺失迹象）、球状星团光度函数（GCLF）和恒星年龄均与NGC 1052-DF2/DF4类似，支持‘子弹矮星’碰撞形成模型；但二者间距更小、相对速度更低，提示该类星系可能具有多样化的演化状态。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 检验‘子弹矮星’模型是否能解释NGC 1052-DF2/DF4类暗物质缺失、球状星团过亮星系的形成，并寻找更多此类系统的观测证据。

Method: 利用VLT/MUSE积分场光谱对FCC 224和FCC 240进行深度观测，分析其恒星种群、内部运动学及球状星团系统，并结合标准质量估计器评估其暗物质含量。

Result: 两星系均表现出低速度弥散、由恒星主导的动力学、异常明亮的球状星团（GCLF呈顶端加厚）、约10 Gyr的共同时期恒星年龄；其投影距离仅75 kpc、相对速度仅16 km/s，显著小于DF2/DF4（240 kpc, 358 km/s）。

Conclusion: FCC 224/FCC 240是‘子弹矮星’模型的有力候选体，支持该机制可产生暗物质贫乏且球状星团过亮的星系；但其更致密的构型表明此类系统可能存在不同演化阶段或环境依赖性，为理论模型提供新约束。

Abstract: The recent "bullet-dwarf" model proposes that high-velocity collisions between dwarf galaxies can produce stellar systems with overluminous globular clusters (GCs) and a deficiency of dark matter, as observed in the NGC 1052 group galaxies NGC 1052-DF2 and NGC 1052-DF4. We present a possible analogue system in the outskirts of the Fornax cluster: the ultra-diffuse galaxy FCC 224 and its close companion FCC 240. Using deep VLT/MUSE integral-field spectroscopy, we characterize their stellar populations, internal kinematics, and GC systems to test this formation scenario. Both galaxies exhibit low velocity dispersions. Interpreted with a standard mass estimator at the half light radius, and allowing for the known limitations associated with flattened systems, their inner dynamics are more naturally explained by stars alone than by either cuspy or cored dark matter halos. Both systems host unusually luminous GCs, closely resembling the top-heavy GCLF of the NGC 1052 pair. Moreover, FCC 224 and FCC 240 are coeval with each other, with mass-weighted stellar ages of ~10 Gyr, and their GC populations share similarly old ages, in agreement with predictions of the formation scenario. Despite these similarities, FCC 224 and FCC 240 form a much tighter system than DF2 and DF4, with a projected separation of 75 kpc (compared to 240 kpc) and a relative velocity of only 16 km/s (compared to 358 km/s). This distinct configuration may suggest a different present-day manifestation of the same general class of galaxies and provides additional observational constraints on models of their formation and evolution.

</details>


### [100] [Resolving galaxy formation in the early Universe with BonFIRE and CampFIRE](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.24104)
*Jenna Samuel,Michael Boylan-Kolchin,Robert Feldmann,Philip Hopkins,Guochao Sun,Pratik Gandhi,Alessandra Venditti,Xuejian Shen,Andrew Wetzel,Jorge Moreno,Julian Munoz,Rachel Cochrane,Claude-Andre Faucher-Giguere,Volker Bromm,Steven Finkelstein,Maria Straight,Connor Painter,Jonathan Stern,James Bullock*

Main category: astro-ph.GA

TL;DR: 本文介绍了BonFIRE和CampFIRE两个高分辨率宇宙学流体动力学模拟，用于研究宇宙黎明时期（z≳6）的星系形成，结合大统计样本与高分辨率优势，预测了星系性质，并揭示了成团性、爆发性恒星形成及高恒星形成效率等关键特征。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 詹姆斯·韦布空间望远镜（JWST）观测到宇宙黎明时期星系数量丰富且增长迅速，挑战现有星系形成模型，亟需新模拟揭示早期星系组装机制。

Method: 基于FIRE-3物理模型，开展BonFIRE（大尺度低分辨率）和CampFIRE（小尺度高分辨率）两套宇宙学流体动力学模拟；采用重采样方法融合二者优势，覆盖宽质量动态范围（M⋆ ∼ 10⁴–10¹⁰ M⊙）；引入简化的Pop III恒星形成模型（顶重型初始质量函数）。

Result: 发现星系形成呈现成团性、爆发性恒星形成；高质晕中恒星形成效率达10–30%，部分低质晕也达>1%并形成超致密星系；UV光度函数在M_UV ≳ −19与观测一致，但在更亮端略高估；UV光度变异性在低质量晕中以晕间弥散主导，在M_halo ≳ 10¹⁰ M⊙时时间爆发性贡献相当；Pop III模型结果与独立预测及观测约束基本一致。

Conclusion: 该模拟表明早期星系形成受高效、非稳态恒星形成过程主导，尤其在特定质量范围内；模拟框架能较好再现JWST观测的关键统计特征，为理解宇宙黎明星系演化提供了重要理论支撑。

Abstract: The abundance and rapid growth of galaxies at cosmic dawn revealed by the James Webb Space Telescope challenges models of galaxy formation, motivating new simulations to uncover the processes driving early galaxy assembly. We present the first results from BonFIRE ($L\approx40$ cMpc, $m_{\rm baryon}\approx5\times10^4~\rm{M}_{\odot}$) and CampFIRE ($L\approx5$ cMpc, at both $m_{\rm baryon}\approx800~\rm{M}_{\odot}$ and $\approx6\times10^3~\rm{M}_{\odot}$), a suite of cosmological hydrodynamic simulations of early galaxy formation ($z\gtrsim6$) from the Feedback In Realistic Environments (FIRE) project, using the FIRE-3 model. We use a resampling procedure to combine the large statistics of BonFIRE with the higher resolution of CampFIRE and robustly predict galaxy properties over a wide dynamic range ($M_{\star}\sim10^4-10^{10}~\rm{M}_{\odot}$). Galaxy formation in this suite emerges through clustered, bursty star formation, with halo-scale star formation efficiencies reaching $10-30\%$ in high-mass halos. A subset of low-mass halos also have surprisingly high efficiencies of $\gtrsim1\%$ and host ultra-compact galaxies with narrow age spreads. We predict galaxy UV luminosity functions at $9\lesssim~z\lesssim25$ in broad agreement with observations at $M_{\rm UV}\gtrsim-19$, with a faint-end turnover at $M_{\rm UV}\approx-14$, but we slightly overpredict the abundance of brighter galaxies. We find that UV luminosity variability in early galaxies is strongly mass-dependent, with halo-to-halo scatter dominating at low masses and contributing comparably to rapid temporal burstiness at $M_{\rm halo}\gtrsim10^{10}~\rm{M}_{\odot}$. We also present first results from a simple Pop~III model with a top-heavy IMF, demonstrating broad agreement with independent Pop~III predictions and observational constraints.

### [101] [The Lumina Project: The Demographics of Active Galactic Nuclei from Quasars to Little Red Dots at $z\geq 3$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.24112)
*Xuejian Shen,Oliver Zier,Aaron Smith,Rongrong Liu,Rahul Kannan,Teodora-Elena Bulichi,Sonja M. Koehler,Volker Springel,Mark Vogelsberger,Lars Hernquist,Rohan P. Naidu,Anna de Graaff,Elia Pizzati,David M. Alexander,Luis C. Ho,Vasily Kokorev,Gene Leung,Anna-Christina Eilers,Ryan C. Hickox*

Main category: astro-ph.GA

TL;DR: 本研究利用Lumina宇宙学辐射流体动力学模拟，预测了z≥3高红移活动星系核（AGN）的多波段光度函数，涵盖从硬X射线到中红外，并成功统一解释了JWST发现的‘小红点’（LRDs）与传统类星体观测。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 高红移AGN是研究早期黑洞增长、星系形成和星系际介质（IGM）演化的重要探针；亟需在统一宇宙学框架下建模包括LRDs在内的高红移AGN整体种群。

Method: 基于大体积（500 cMpc）³、高分辨率（2×6000³）的Lumina模拟，自洽追踪数亿个星系与超大质量黑洞（SMBHs）及其对IGM电离与热状态的影响；构建经验模型，将模拟SMBH映射至观测AGN，引入吸积光度弥散与LRD相位占空比（30%）等关键参数。

Result: 成功再现LRDs的光度函数与成团性；复现了JWST前类星体光度函数（需~0.3 dex对数正态光度弥散）；定量给出AGN/LRD数密度与黑洞质量密度的红移演化；确认该AGN种群主导模拟中的HeII再电离。

Conclusion: 所提经验AGN模型为在统一宇宙学框架下开展高红移AGN（含LRDs）的普适种群合成建模奠定了基础。

Abstract: High-redshift active galactic nuclei (AGN) serve as powerful probes of early black-hole growth, galaxy formation, and the evolving intergalactic medium (IGM). In this work, we use Lumina, a cosmological radiation-hydrodynamic simulation spanning the epochs of hydrogen and helium reionization, which combines a large $(500\,{\rm cMpc})^3$ volume with $2\times 6000^3$ resolution elements, to explore high-redshift AGN. The simulation self-consistently follows hundreds of millions of galaxies and supermassive black holes (SMBHs), together with their impact on the ionization and thermal state of the IGM. We exploit this uniquely large dynamic range to predict multi-band AGN luminosity functions (LFs) at $z \geq 3$, from hard X-rays to the mid-infrared. These predictions encompass both moderately luminous quasars and the faint ``Little Red Dots'' (LRDs) uncovered by JWST. We develop an empirical model that maps simulated SMBHs onto observed AGN using bolometric and extinction/absorption corrections for canonical AGN and LRDs, and in which SMBHs with $M_{\rm BH}\leq 10\,M_{\rm seed} \sim 10^{7}\,{\rm M}_{\odot}$ stay in the LRD phase with a duty cycle of $30\%$. This simple framework reproduces the observed LFs and clustering of LRDs. Meanwhile, the pre-JWST quasar LF constraints are recovered, although we find that a $\sim 0.3$ dex log-normal scatter in bolometric luminosity is required to reproduce the bright end. We place the simulated AGN population in the cosmological context by quantifying the redshift evolution of AGN and LRD number densities, and their contributions to the integrated BH mass densities. The same AGN population is the dominant driver for the HeII reionization modelled self-consistently in Lumina. This empirical AGN model paves the way for general population-synthesis models of high-redshift AGN, including LRDs, in a unified cosmological framework.

</details>


### [102] [A Redshift-based Red Selection of Dusty Star-forming Galaxies](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.24264)
*A. J. Barger,L. L. Cowie,S. J. McKay,F. E. Bauer*

Main category: astro-ph.GA

TL;DR: 本文利用JWST和ALMA对星系团A2744的观测，发现红光（f_J/f_V > 3）星系主要为尘埃遮蔽的恒星形成星系（DSFGs）、小红点（LRDs）和宁静星系；红光选择高效识别ALMA探测到的DSFGs，但未探测到LRDs或宁静星系；多数高光度红源为DSFGs，少数低红移宁静星系可通过UVJ图识别；约10% DSFGs受AGN主导，且几乎所有DSFGs和宁静星系恒星质量均高于10^10太阳质量，该质量阈值在z>5时显著减少。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解高红移（z=1.5–5.5）下红光星系的物理性质与分类，特别是区分尘埃遮蔽恒星形成星系（DSFGs）、小红点（LRDs）和宁静星系，并检验多波段颜色选择的有效性。

Method: 结合JWST（1.5–4.44微米）与ALMA（870微米/1.2毫米）对星系团A2744的深度观测，利用rest-frame f_J/f_V > 3颜色选择红光星系，并通过ALMA探测、形态分析（延展vs致密）、UVJ图及X射线数据进行分类与证认。

Result: 红光选择识别出83%的显著ALMA源（34/41）；高光度红源多为延展DSFGs，低光度者多为致密LRDs；未在ALMA中探测到LRDs或宁静星系；大部分延展红源为DSFGs，少量低红移宁静星系由UVJ图确认；~10% DSFGs具高X射线光度，属AGN主导；几乎所有DSFGs与宁静星系M_star > 10^10 M_sun，该质量星系在z>5急剧减少。

Conclusion: rest-frame红光（f_J/f_V > 3）是高效识别高红移DSFGs的示踪器，但无法有效捕获LRDs与宁静星系；DSFGs与宁静星系共享高恒星质量特征，其宇宙学密度在z>5迅速下降，反映大质量星系形成早期的剧烈演化。

Abstract: We use JWST observations (1.5 micron to 4.44 micron), together with complete ALMA observations (870 micron and/or 1.2 mm), of the massive lensing cluster field A2744 to show that galaxies between z=1.5 and z=5.5 with rest-frame red colors f_J/f_V > 3 correspond to dusty star-forming galaxies (DSFGs), little red dots (LRDs), and quiescent galaxies. The color selection picks out 34 of the 41 >4.5-sigma ALMA sources in the field (83%). We find that the luminous red sources are generally extended, while the less luminous red sources are almost all compact and correspond to the LRD population. We also find that the great majority of the luminous, extended red sources are DSFGs based on the ALMA data, with a small admixture of quiescent galaxies at z<3-4 that we identify based on their location in the rest-frame U-V versus V-J diagram. We do not detect any LRDs or quiescent galaxies at the >3-sigma level in the ALMA images. Roughly 10% of the DSFGs have high rest-frame X-ray luminosities and must be AGN dominated. The DSFGs and quiescent galaxies nearly all have M_star>10^{10} solar masses. These massive galaxies become rare at z>5, paralleling the fall off in the number of detected DSFGs.

</details>


### [103] [The 3D Structure and Kinematics of the Local Disk-Halo Interface: Intermediate-velocity Clouds are the Minority of High-altitude Clouds in the Solar Neighborhood](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.24342)
*Theo J. O'Neill,Andrew K. Saydjari,Catherine Zucker,Eric W. Koch,Robert A. Benjamin,Philipp Frank,Stephanie Yoshida*

Main category: astro-ph.GA

TL;DR: 本研究利用三维尘埃图首次在太阳邻域的盘-晕界面进行三维空间搜索，识别出1695个尘埃云，并构建了519个具有高置信度距离、三维形态和径向速度的样本；发现IVCs仅占高海拔云的18%，且存在显著南北不对称性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统上基于径向速度识别盘-晕界面的异常速度气体（如IVCs和HVCs），但缺乏三维空间信息限制了对其物理性质的准确测量；本文旨在利用最新三维尘埃图实现对本地盘-晕界面气体结构的三维表征。

Method: 应用拓扑结构识别方法于秒差距分辨率的三维尘埃图，识别太阳附近1.25 kpc内的尘埃云；结合HI 21 cm辐射形态相似性评估云的动力学性质；构建具有高置信度距离、三维形态和径向速度的云样本。

Result: 识别出1695个尘埃云（z = -646 pc 至 +928 pc），其中519个具有高置信度三维参数；首次在三维中定位多个IVCs，获得其距离、尺寸、密度、质量、压强和尘气比；发现高海拔（|z| ≥ 480 pc）云分布存在显著北/南不对称性（北天是南天的2.9倍），且IVCs仅占该区域云总数的18%。

Conclusion: 低径向速度云在本地盘-晕界面中占主导，凸显在建模星系喷泉流和反馈过程时必须纳入这类结构；三维尘埃图极大提升了对盘-晕界面多相介质结构和动力学的理解。

Abstract: Studies of the Milky Way's disk-halo interface have historically identified inflowing and outflowing gas incompatible with disk rotation on the basis of radial velocity, leading to the well-known categories of intermediate-velocity clouds (IVCs) and high-velocity clouds (HVCs). In this work, we leverage recent progress in 3D dust mapping of the Solar Neighborhood to perform the first 3D spatial search for anomalous-velocity clouds at the local disk-halo interface. We identify 1,695 dust clouds within 1.25 kpc of the Sun (with altitudes ranging between z=-646 pc to z=+928 pc) by applying a topological structure finding method to a parsec-resolution 3D dust map. We then evaluate the morphological similarity between these clouds and HI 21 cm emission to measure cloud kinematics, and construct a sample of 519 clouds with high-confidence distances, 3D morphologies, and radial velocities. Among these are several IVCs (embedded within the well-known Intermediate Velocity Arch complex) now identified in 3D for the first time, enabling direct measurement of their distances, sizes, densities, masses, pressures, and dust-to-gas ratios. We observe a pronounced asymmetry in the vertical distribution of all clouds in the Solar Neighborhood, with $(2.9 \pm 0.2) \times$ more clouds in the Northern Galactic hemisphere than the Southern above altitudes at which IVCs are present ($|z| \geq 480$ pc). IVCs make up only 18% of the total number of clouds located at these high altitudes, with the remainder having low velocities -- highlighting the importance of accounting for low-radial-velocity structures when evaluating the local disk-halo interface and modeling feedback-driven Galactic fountain flows.

### [104] [Changing-look Active Galactic Nuclei from SDSS, LAMOST and DESI Survey](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.24429)
*Guohai Chen,Wenxin Yang,Xuhong Ye,Zhiqiang Chen,Zhiyuan Pei,Hubing Xiao,Junhui Fan*

Main category: astro-ph.GA

TL;DR: 本文通过交叉匹配SDSS、LAMOST和DESI光谱数据，系统搜寻变脸活动星系核（CLAGNs），发现45个CLAGNs（含40个新源）及其中12个重复变脸源（RCLAGNs），支持CL行为源于反复的吸积率变化或盘不稳定性，并揭示RCLAGNs呈现高-低-高吸积态演化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管已报道千余个光学变脸活动星系核（CLAGNs），其物理起源仍不清楚，且重复变脸源（RCLAGNs）极为稀少；扩大CLAGN样本尤其是RCLAGNs，对约束其物理机制至关重要。

Method: 系统交叉匹配SDSS与LAMOST光谱数据搜寻CLAGNs，并利用DESI第三期光谱检验重复变脸行为；结合黑洞质量与爱丁顿比分析吸积态演化；估算变脸时间尺度的观测上限。

Result: 发现45个CLAGNs（40个为新源），以关断事件为主（43个关断、2个开启）；识别出12个RCLAGNs；RCLAGNs在MBH–Lbol/LEdd图中呈现清晰的高-低-高吸积态演化；首次与第二次变脸的静止帧时间上限分别约为10年和4年。

Conclusion: 高比例RCLAGNs表明CL行为可能源于反复发生的物理过程（如吸积率涨落或吸积盘不稳定性）；RCLAGNs的吸积态演化进一步证实CL现象与吸积功率的周期性变化密切相关；观测时间基线主导了测得的变脸时间上限差异，而非真实物理时标差异。

Abstract: Although more than 1000 optical changing-look active galactic nuclei (CLAGNs) have been reported to date, their physical origin remains unclear, and repeating CLAGNs (RCLAGNs) are still rare. Expanding the CLAGN sample, especially RCLAGNs, is therefore important for constraining the underlying mechanism. We systematically search for CLAGNs by cross-matching spectroscopic observations from the Sloan Digital Sky Survey (SDSS) and the Large Sky Area Multi-Object Fiber Spectroscopic Telescope (LAMOST), and further use spectra from the Dark Energy Spectroscopic Instrument (DESI) to investigate repeating CL behavior. We identify 45 CLAGNs, including 40 newly reported sources. The sample is dominated by turn-off events, with 43 turn-off and 2 turn-on sources, possibly because Type 2 AGNs either lack a detectable broad-line region or have their broad emission lines obscured by circumnuclear dust. Using DESI as a third spectroscopic epoch, we identify 12 RCLAGNs. This high detection rate of repeated CL behavior suggests that CL transitions may arise from recurrent physical processes, such as accretion-rate fluctuations or disk instabilities. In the log MBH - log(Lbol/LEdd) plane, RCLAGNs further show a clear high-low-high accretion-state evolution, supporting a close link between CL behavior and recurrent changes in accretion power. Finally, the rest-frame upper limits on the transition timescales are about 10 yr for the first transition and about 4 yr for the second, reflecting different survey time baselines rather than intrinsic differences in physical transition timescales.

### [105] [FASTAR -- II. Semi-resolved evolutionary stellar population models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.24476)
*Ignacio Martín-Navarro,Alexandre Vazdekis,Luis Peralta de Arriba,Isaac Alonso Asensio,Patricia Iglesias Navarro,Eirini Angeloudi,Francesco La Barbera,Miguel Cerviño,Katja Fahrion,Tereza Jerabkova,Michael A. Beasley,Jesús Falcón-Barroso,Marc Huertas-Company,Sebastián F. Sánchez,Prashin Jethwa*

Main category: astro-ph.GA

TL;DR: 本文提出了半解析版FASTAR模型，用于处理恒星初始质量函数（IMF）未完全采样的情况，适用于高空间分辨率和低表面亮度观测，具有随机性、宽年龄/金属丰度范围及高效JAX计算支持。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前高分辨率与低表面亮度观测使得传统完全采样IMF的假设不再普适，需发展能刻画离散采样IMF随机行为的星族合成模型。

Method: 在原有FASTAR积分模型基础上，构建半解析版本，引入恒星数量对等时线各演化阶段的实际采样效应，实现IMF随机抽样，并支持JAX加速计算。

Result: 提供了20 Myr–14 Gyr年龄、[M/H]∈(-2.5, +0.3)金属丰度、多种IMF形式的半解析模型；覆盖3540–7400 Å高分辨率光谱与2000–12000 Å低分辨率SED；揭示了等效宽度、颜色、质光比等观测量因IMF采样不足而呈现显著随机偏差。

Conclusion: 半解析FASTAR模型突破了完全采样IMF的限制，其固有随机性模糊了模型预测与观测数据的边界，推动基于采样统计的新型推断方法发展。

Abstract: Standard evolutionary synthesis models rely on the assumption of a fully sampled stellar initial mass function (IMF). Under this assumption, the age, chemical composition, and IMF uniquely define the predicted absorption spectra. However, with current instrumentation pushing observations towards higher spatial resolutions and lower surface brightnesses, the assumption of a fully sampled IMF does not always hold true. Here we present the semi-resolved version of the FASTAR models, a comprehensive set of evolutionary synthesis predictions able to reproduce the stochastic behavior of discretely-sampled IMFs. Semi-resolved FASTAR predictions share the same evolutionary principles, ingredients, and features of the integral (fully sampled IMF) version of the FASTAR models, expanding a range of ages from 20 Myr to 14 Gyr, metallicities between -2.5 < [M/H] < +0.3, and several IMF functional forms. Detailed spectroscopic measurements can be carried out within the 3,540-7,400 A wavelength range, and low-resolution spectral energy distributions can also be synthesized over a wider 2,000-to-12,000 A coverage. Semi-resolved FASTAR models also depend on the number of stars contributing to the observed spectra, which determines the effective sampling of the different stellar evolutionary phases along the isochrones. This incomplete sampling implies that semi-resolved FASTAR models are inevitably stochastic. On top of the inherent stochasticity of the models, derived quantities such as equivalent widths, colors, or mass-to-light ratios might present strong deviations compared to standard fully sampled simple stellar population models. This stochasticity dilutes the boundary between model predictions and data, promoting new sampling-based inference approaches. FASTAR semi-resolved models allow for the effective exploration of the parameter space thanks to their optimized, JAX-based computation.

### [106] [A Three-Decade VLBI Study of the Nucleus in the Lobe-Dominated Quasar 3C207](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.24746)
*D. H. Hough,J. P. Linick,E. L. Danielson,S. M. Escobedo,H. D. Ibaroudene,B. D. Sadler,N. A. Polito,R. C. Vermeulen,C. E. Aars,C. L. Newton,T. A. Rector*

Main category: astro-ph.GA

TL;DR: 本文通过长达29年的VLBI观测，研究了类星体3C207核区的射电喷流结构与动力学行为，发现其存在准周期爆发、喷流进动及再准直过程，并支持喷流在小张角圆锥面上弹道运动的物理模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为检验相对论性喷流模型在不同喷流取向角下的适用性，选取3CR样本中最强且最变的lobe-dominated quasar（LDQ）3C207作为研究对象。

Method: 利用1981–2010年间在X波段（8.4/10.7 GHz）开展的甚长基线干涉测量（VLBI）观测，分析高分辨率（~0.5–1.0 mas）、高灵敏度（~0.1–0.2 mJy beam⁻¹）图像中的核区光变、成分运动学、位置角演化及喷流形态。

Result: 发现核区约每7年发生一次流量爆发；存在一个静止‘真实核’和一个向东摆动的成分，其位置角长期增加约40°并伴有短期约10°反转；喷流呈单侧弯曲结构，延伸约25 mas，成分视横向速度达~10c，其中一成分在2–3 mas处由7c加速至14c，另一成分显示可能减速；成分持续膨胀直至到达再准直区。

Conclusion: 观测结果支持3C207具有准周期爆发、喷流在小张角圆锥面上的弹道进动，以及发生在~100 pc尺度上的再准直过程，该过程影响成分运动并收窄圆锥几何结构。

Abstract: We present results from very-long-baseline-interferometry (VLBI) observations of the nucleus in the lobe-dominated quasar 3C207. These observations were completed at 8.4 or 10.7 GHz (X-band) from 1981 to 2010, spanning 29 years. The nucleus of 3C207 is the strongest and most variable in the 3CR complete sample of LDQs, which is under study to test relativistic jet models over a wide range of jet orientation angles. Images have typical resolutions of ~0.5-1.0 milliarcseconds (mas) and sensitivities of ~0.1-0.2 mJy beam^{-1}. The VLBI core region has flux density outbursts at mean intervals of ~7 yr; two of these are multiple outbursts from a stationary "true: core that feeds a "swinging component" ~0.5 mas to the east. The position angle (PA) of the swinging component shows a long-term increase of ~40°, with a short-term reversal of ~10°. A one-sided, curved VLBI jet extends ~25 mas eastward, with components spanning a PA range of ~25°. The jet components have average apparent transverse velocities ~10c. One component shows apparent acceleration from 7c to 14c at 2-3 mas from the true core, where the flow is redirected toward PA ~90°. Another component shows marginal evidence for apparent deceleration. Individual jet components expand until reaching the recollimation zone. Our results are consistent with a physical model in which 3C207 has quasi-periodic outbursts, jet precession by ballistic components on a conical surface with a small opening angle, and a recollimation process that modifies component motions and narrows the conical geometry on a scale of ~100 pc.

### [107] [Puzzling Ultra-Diffuse Galaxy Evolution (PUDGE). II. A transformation pathway from UDGs to compact dwarfs (CDs) in galaxy clusters](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.24918)
*Nataša Pavlov,Ana Mitrašinović*

Main category: astro-ph.GA

TL;DR: 本文利用IllustrisTNG模拟研究超弥散星系（UDGs）向致密矮星系（CDs）的演化路径，发现部分CDs起源于高气体含量的UDG前身，在落入星系团过程中经历剧烈星暴形成致密恒星核，而非传统认为的潮汐剥离暴露原有核；该过程依赖环境与气体丰度，揭示了一种全新的、由星系团驱动的转化机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 观测发现UDGs与CDs在星系团中空间分布呈显著反相关，暗示二者可能存在演化联系；传统观点认为CDs是UDGs经潮汐剥离后暴露原有致密核所致，但该假说隐含‘致密核必须在并入星系团前即已存在’的前提，本文旨在检验该前提是否成立。

Method: 基于IllustrisTNG宇宙学模拟（TNG100），在7个星系团中识别UDG和CD样本，对117个当前CDs进行回溯追踪，分析其结构演化、气体分数、恒星形成历史及空间轨道，重点考察其是否曾经历UDG相及其物理条件。

Result: 确认TNG100再现观测到的UDG–CD空间反相关；发现8个CDs的前身曾短暂处于UDG相，具有极高气体分数（fgas ≳ 0.8），且其大部分恒星质量及峰值恒星形成率均发生在最大空间尺度之后；这些UDG前身并不存在显著恒星核，表明CD的致密结构是在剥离过程中新形成的。

Conclusion: UDGs可经星系团环境触发的星暴活动转化为CDs，该转化路径不依赖预先存在的致密核，而是由高气体含量驱动、在环境作用下实时构建致密恒星结构，是一种区别于经典潮汐剥离的新机制。

Abstract: Ultra-diffuse galaxies (UDGs) and compact dwarfs (CDs) occupy opposite extremes of the structural parameter space of dwarf galaxies, yet their spatial distributions in clusters suggest a possible evolutionary connection. Observational studies have reported a pronounced anti-correlation between the two populations, interpreted as evidence that CDs represent tidally stripped remnants of diffuse progenitors, a scenario that implicitly assumes a compact stellar nucleus must be present at infall to survive environmental processing. We test this hypothesis using the IllustrisTNG cosmological simulation (TNG100) by examining the UDG and CD populations in seven galaxy clusters and tracing the evolutionary histories of 117 present-day CDs. We confirm that TNG100 reproduces the observed spatial anti-correlation, with CDs concentrated within $d/R_{200} \lesssim 0.2$ and UDGs preferentially inhabiting the cluster outskirts. Tracing CDs back in time, we identify eight systems whose progenitors undergo a transient UDG phase, with extremely high gas fractions ($f_{\rm gas} \gtrsim 0.8$), immediately before cluster infall. In all eight systems, a vast majority of the present-day stellar mass was assembled after the epoch of maximum spatial extent, and the peak star formation rate (SFR) during the transformation is the highest each galaxy achieves across its entire lifetime. The UDG progenitors show no prominent stellar cores before infall, demonstrating that the compact component of the resulting CD is not an exposed pre-existing nucleus but is instead freshly built through starburst-driven star formation during the stripping process itself. Our results reveal a physically motivated UDG-to-CD transformation pathway driven entirely by cluster environment, fundamentally distinct from classical tidal stripping scenarios, and highlight the critical role of gas richness as a prerequisite for this channel.

### [108] [Small and Complex II: Characterizing the Disk and Stellar Envelope of Edge-on $z \sim 0$ Massive Compact Galaxies](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.25075)
*A. Schnorr-Müller,K. Slodkowski Clerici,F. Pinna,R. Merib-Dias,M. Trevisan,T. V. Ricci,F. Ferrari,A. C. Santiago-Menezes,W. L. Becker,F. Palacios*

Main category: astro-ph.GA

TL;DR: 本文对75个边缘朝向的大质量致密星系（MCGs）进行多成分测光分解，发现其致密性源于 bulge、disk 和 envelope 三部分整体更紧凑，且各成分尺寸相互关联；与对照样本相比，MCGs 具有更小的 bulge 和 envelope、更短更厚的 disk；其 envelope 形状多样，中间椭率成因不明；结果不支持干并合主导形成 envelope，而与遗迹星系结构高度相似，暗示同源演化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解大质量致密星系（MCGs）为何异常致密——是单一结构成分主导，还是多成分协同致密？其外围恒星包层（envelope）的物理本质（如是否为并合遗迹或增厚盘）尚不明确，需通过结构分解厘清。

Method: 基于Hyper Suprime-Cam r波段图像，对75个z<0.1的边缘朝向MCGs开展三成分（bulge+disk+envelope）测光分解；构建质量与红移匹配的非致密S0星系对照样本，系统比较各成分有效半径、标尺长度、轴比、通量占比及椭率等结构参数。

Result: MCGs各结构成分均更紧凑：bulge有效半径（0.3 vs 0.5 kpc）、envelope有效半径（4.4 vs 5.7 kpc）、disk标尺长度（1.1 vs 1.7 kpc）均显著更小，且disk更厚（h_R/z_0 = 3.9 vs 5.3）；bulge/disk通量占比（B/T≈0.3, D/T≈0.4）与对照组相当；envelope椭率跨度大（0–0.7），MCGs整体更圆；成分尺寸强耦合；与8个遗迹星系结构及尺寸-质量关系一致。

Conclusion: MCGs的致密性是bulge、disk和envelope协同收缩的结果，而非单因素导致；envelope的中间椭率成因无法仅由测光判定；尺寸耦合与显著残存disk共同排除干微并合作为envelope主形成机制；MCGs与遗迹星系构成同一结构家族，暗示其可能为早期快速形成后演化停滞的‘化石’系统。

Abstract: We present multi-component photometric decompositions of $r$-band Hyper Suprime-Cam images for a sample of 75 edge-on massive compact galaxies (MCGs) at $z < 0.1$, selected as $+2σ$ outliers in the stellar mass-velocity dispersion relation and $-2σ$ outliers in the velocity dispersion-size relation. MCGs are composed of compact bulges and disks embedded within stellar envelopes of unclear physical nature. Comparing MCGs to a mass- and redshift-matched control sample of non-compact edge-on S0 galaxies with a similar three-component structure, we find that the smaller sizes of MCGs are not driven by a single component. MCGs host more compact bulges and envelopes ($R_\mathrm{e,bulge} \sim 0.3$ versus $0.5$kpc; $R_\mathrm{e,env} \sim 4.4$ versus $5.7$kpc), as well as shorter and thicker disks ($h_R \sim 1.1$ versus $1.7$kpc; $h_R/z_0 \sim 3.9$ versus $5.3$). The sizes of the structural components are coupled, suggesting their formation processes are linked. Median bulge- and disk-to-total flux fractions are similar in both samples, with $B/T \sim 0.3$ and $D/T \sim 0.4$. Envelope ellipticities span $ε_\mathrm{env} \sim 0$-$0.7$, with MCGs exhibiting rounder envelopes. Low- and high-ellipticity envelopes are broadly consistent with stellar halos and thick disks, respectively. However, the nature of intermediate ellipticity envelopes remains ambiguous from photometry alone. The coupling between component sizes, together with the survival of a substantial disk component, argues against dry minor mergers as the dominant envelope-building mechanism. A comparison with 8 relic galaxies reveals that MCGs and relics share similar bulge-disk-envelope structures and follow the same component size-mass relations, consistent with belonging to a common structural family.
